

**** TALK ****
Help talk.   Entries and curr values.  Entries followed by CR or ';'
B<?> Battery assignments.   For example:
  Bm=  0.  Mon chem 0='BB', 1='LI' [0]
  Bs=  0.  Sim chem 0='BB', 1='LI' [0]
  BP=   1.00.  # parallel in bank [ 1.00]'
  BS=   1.00.  # series in bank [ 1.00]'
C<?> Charge assignments.   For example:
  Ca=  set soc in all - '(0-1.1)'
  Cm=  set soc model only (and ekf if modeling)- '(0-1.1)'
D/S<?> Adjustments.   For example:
  Da=  -0.940    : delta amp sense, A [ -0.230]
  Db=  -0.170    : delta noa sense, A [ -0.570]
  Di=   0.000    : delta all sense, A [  0.000]
  Dc=   0.000    : delta sense, V [  0.000]
  Dn= 1.00       : coul eff
  Dp= 400       : publish frame, ms [400]
  Dr= 100       : minor frame, ms [100]
  Dt=   0.000    : delta sense, deg C [  0.000]
  Dv= 0.01       : Table adjust, V [0.01]
  Sc= 1.00       : Scalar model size
  Sh=   1.000    : hysteresis scalar 1e-6 - 100 [1]
  Sr= 1.00       : Scalar res sim
  Sk= 1.00       : Sat model cutback scalar
H<?>   Manage history
  Hd= dump summary log
  HR= reset summary log
  Hs= save and print log
M<?> Amp tweaks
  MC=   0.001    : Amp Coul eff max change allowed scakar [0.001]
  Mk=   1.000    : Amp Coul eff scalar [1]
  Mw=   6.000    : Amp time to wait for next tweak, hr [18]]
  Mx=   0.010    : Amp Coul eff max allowed scalar [0.01]
  Mz=   8.528    : Amp time since last tweak, hr [varies]
N<?> No amp tweaks
  NC=   0.001    : No Amp Coul eff max change allowed scakar [0.001]
  Nk=   1.000    : No Amp Coul eff scalar [1]
  Nw=   6.000    : No Amp time to wait for next tweak, hr [18]]
  Nx=   0.010    : Amp Coul eff max allowed scalar [0.01]
  Nz=   8.528    : No Amp time since last tweak, hr [varies]
P<?>   Print Battery values
  Pa= all
  Pc= all coulombs
  Pe= ekf
  Pm= monitor
  PM= amp tweak
  PN= no amp tweak
  Pr= retained and command
  Ps= simulation
  Pt= all state-space
  Px= current signal selection
  Pv= voltage signal details
Q      vital stats
R<?>   Reset
  Re= equalize delta_q in Sim to Mon
  Rh= reset all hys
  Ri= reset all delta_q_inf
  Rr= saturate battery monitor and equalize Sim & Mon
  RR= saturate, equalize, & nominalize all testing for DEPLOY
  Rs= small reset.  Reset flags to reinitialize filters
s   curr signal select (0=amp preferred, 1=noamp) = 0
v=  0    : verbosity, -128 - +128. [2]
    -<>:   Negative - Arduino plot compatible
    v-1:   GP Arduino plot
     v4:   GP
  +/-v5:   OLED display
     v6:   EKF solver iter during init
     v7:   EKF solver summary during init
    v-7:   Battery i/o Arduino plot
     v8:   Randles state space init
   v-11:   Summary Arduino
 +/-v12:   EKF
 +/-v14:   vshunt and Ibatt raw
    v15:   vb raw
 +/-v34:   EKF detailed
   v-35:   EKF summary Arduino
    v35:   Randles balance
 +/-v37:   EKF short
   v-41:   Inj
    v75:   voc_low check model
    v76:   vb model
 +/-v78:   Batt model saturation
    v79:   sat_ib model
 +/-v96:   CC saturation
 +/-v97:   CC model saturation
w   turn on wifi = 0
W<?>  - seconds to wait
X<?> - Test Mode.   For example:
  Xd= 0,   dc-dc charger on [0]
  Xm= 0,   modeling bitmap [000]
       0x8 tweak_test = 0
       0x4 current = 0
       0x2 voltage = 0
       0x1 temp = 0
  Xa=   0.000  : Inj amp A pk (0-18.3) [0]
  Xf=   0.000  : Inj freq Hz (0-2) [0]
  Xt= 0  : Inj type.  'c', 's', 'q', 't' (cos, sine, square, tri)
  Xo=   0.000  : Inj inj_bias A (-18.3-18.3) [0]
  Di=   0.000  : Inj  A (unlimited) [0]
  Xp= <?>, programmed inj settings...
      Xp-1:  Off, modeling false
      Xp0:  steady-state modeling
      Xp1:  1 Hz sine about 0
      Xp2:  1 Hz square about 0
      Xp3:  1 Hz triangle about 0
      Xp4:  -1C soft discharge, reset xp0 or Di0
      Xp5:  +1C soft charge
      Xp6:  +0.2C hard charge
      Xp8:  1 Hz cosine about 0
      Xp9:  silent tweak reg test
      Xp10:  tweak reg test
      Xp11:  slow cycle reg test
      Xp20:  tweak-like data collection
      Xp21:  slow data collection
  XC=   0.000 cycles inj
  XR  RUN inj
  XS  STOP inj
  XW= 2779096.58 s wait start inj
h   this menu
